msg:First of all, the hotel has a beautiful environment. It covers a large area, the lobby is spacious, the room area is ample, and the environment is quiet. Open the window to enjoy the scenery, the lush scenery in front of you, the birds and insects are chirping, and you can also enjoy the peacocks while eating in the restaurant, which makes people feel very comfortable and cozy. Second, the service is warm and thoughtful. Check in and help with luggage enthusiastically; not only upgraded the room type for free, but also tried to arrange it nearby for our three families; every day, yogurt and small biscuits are given intimately; the restaurant staff are very enthusiastic, and Fang Fangyuan and Cao Qin are praised by name; one night, I ordered takeout and found that there were not enough chopsticks. I asked the restaurant for help and gave disposable chopsticks and vinegar very readily; the uncle at the swimming pool was also very enthusiastic to provide various help. Third, the hotel facilities are complete. The bedding in the room is clean and comfortable, the bathroom area is sufficient, and a long clothesline is set up in a particularly humane way. The curtains, TV lights, and Xiaodu can be used in the room. There is also a swimming pool and gym on the first floor. Although there are only two or three children in the swimming pool, there are also lifeguards who are conscientiously guarding, and the restaurant food is delicious. If there is any shortcoming, it should be that the hotel is far from the city center. If you want to order takeout, it takes an average of one hour. In short, I am very satisfied with this hotel and give it 5 stars.

posted:Posted February 24, 2024
msg:Quality evaluation
During the Spring Festival holiday, I brought my family to Lianyungang for a tour. I took Huaguoshan Scenic Area as a must-see tourist attraction, so I chose Huaguoshan Hotel without hesitation. We were not disappointed when we checked in. The hotel covers a large area, parking is convenient, and there are charging parking spaces (the management is not in place, and people leave after the car is parked). The hotel lobby is magnificent, and the front desk staff are professional and enthusiastic, efficient, polite and thoughtful. After going through the formalities, there are service staff to guide you to the room, which is considerate. The room is spacious and bright, with a cloakroom, a separate bathroom, a clothesline, and a bathtub. After visiting the scenic area, you can take a bath after being tired and relax. There is a Chinese restaurant on the second floor of the hotel. You can order dishes or set meals. The set meals are a combination of meat and vegetables, and the quantity is sufficient and delicious. The set meals for 2-3 people are enough for four adults to eat well. Breakfast is on the first floor of the hotel, with rich content, and you can enjoy peacocks while eating breakfast. The waiter who provides clear soup noodles and wontons is very enthusiastic. A five-star hotel experience with a very high credibility and value ratio.

The room is large, with a dressing room, a bathtub, and separate wet and dry bathrooms. The service is also good. When I checked in, I saw that I had a lot of luggage and helped me leave it at the door. After cleaning, yogurt and biscuits were also given.

breakfast:

Xiao Qin, the waiter at the restaurant's front desk, is very warm and thoughtful. The food comes out quickly and the plates are collected quickly.

bed:

The hotel recreation center has table tennis, gym, and swimming pool. The water temperature is a bit cold, but everything else is fine. The service was also very considerate. One of us forgot to wear a swimming cap, and the front desk lent us one. Just remember to return it before leaving.
